## THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA


## PREAMBLE

WE, THE PEOPLE OF INDIA, having solemnly resolved to constitute India into a *[SOVEREIGN SOCIALIST SECULAR DEMOCRATIC REPUBLIC] and to secure to allits citizens :

JUSTICE, social, economic and S: political; si LIBERTY of thought, expression, belief, | | faith and worship;


## EQUALITY of status and of opportunity;

and to promote among them all NS

FRATERNITY assuring the dignity of | /..


## the individual and the “[unity and [


## integrity of the Nation]; ‘

IN OUR CONSTITUENT ASSEMBLY |- this twenty-sixth day of November, 1949 do | .. HEREBY ADOPT, ENACT AND GIVE TO |}. OURSELVES THIS CONSTITUTION. .

1. Subs. by the Constitution (Forty-second Amendment) Act, 1976, Sec.2, for "Sovereign Democratic Republic" (w.e.f. 3.1.1977)

2. Subs. by the Constitution (Forty-second Amendment) Act, 1976, Sec.2, for "Unity of the Nation" (w.e.f. 3.1.1977)
